üí•**Update**: Papers accepted by [ICSE 2026 First Cycle](https://Conference.researchr.org/track/icse-2026/icse-2026-research-track) are included in this list!

# Paper List of SE Conferences

Research papers accepted by {ICSE, FSE, ASE, ISSTA} since 2020.

### How to Contribute
1. Fork this repository and clone it: `git clone https://github.com/iCSawyer/SEConfPaperList`
2. Install the dependencies: `pip install scrapy openpyxl`
3. Add new links in `paper_spider/utils/paperlist.py`
4. Run and push: `scrapy crawl paper_spider`
